*[RAM]unique[0x1080:3] = unique[0x1090:2]

unique[0x7c0:3] = 0xff << 0xc
unique[0x7e0:3] = unique[0x7c0:3] | 0x2a9
unique[0xc50:1] = *[RAM]unique[0x7e0:3]
B = unique[0xc50:1]
unique[0x9ae0:1] = CCR & 0xfb
unique[0x9ad0:1] = B == 0x0
unique[0x9af0:1] = unique[0x9ad0:1] << 0x2
CCR = unique[0x9ae0:1] | unique[0x9af0:1]
unique[0x9b10:1] = CCR & 0xf7
unique[0x9b00:1] = B s< 0x0
unique[0x9b20:1] = unique[0x9b00:1] << 0x3
CCR = unique[0x9b10:1] | unique[0x9b20:1]
unique[0x16e0:1] = CCR & 0xfd
unique[0x16f0:1] = 0x0 << 0x1
CCR = unique[0x16e0:1] | unique[0x16f0:1]
